This lesson helps students discover the power of rereading for themselves as they read a short, challenging poem.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003ENoticing What You Notice with Poetry\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E guides students through the process of reading and rereading a complex poem 3 times – rating and reflecting on their comprehension each time – to learn the value of rereading, reflection, metacognition, and text-based discussion in understanding challenging poems. The prompts and questions lead students to considering multiple interpretations and to revise their understanding as they make meaning from a complex poem.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cbr \u002F\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EWhat's Included\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E*  Detailed lesson plan with teacher notes and questions for leading a class discussion to debrief the activity\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E* Six-page note catcher with prompts and questions for students to record their thinking as they read, rate, reflect, and reread the poem\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E* Exit ticket for students to reflect on their learning and how they will apply it in the future\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003E* Now includes the option to assign as an \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.easelbytpt.com\u002F\" target=\"_blank\"\u003EEasel by TpT™\u003C\u002Fa\u003E Activity!\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EHow It Works\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EA six-page note catcher structures the lesson, leading students through a series of readings and reflections that encourage and support them to engage in the dynamic, multi-faceted process of creating meaning from a challenging poem.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EThe reflective and metacognitive question prompts, as well as the small group discussion, whole class debrief, and exit ticket reflection help students become more aware of their own reading process and identify the cognitive skills and approaches to reading that will help them make sense of complex poems in the future.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003ELesson Overview\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E1. Students read the same poem three times. With each reading, they rate their understanding and reflect on how they made sense of the poem as they were reading.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E2. Students respond to metacognitive questions and capture their thinking on a “Noticing What You Notice” note catcher.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E3. Next, in small groups students share what they noticed about themselves as readers and about their understanding of the poem over the course of their three readings.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E4. Then, students engage in a whole class discussion to debrief the experience.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E5. Finally, students complete an exit ticket reflecting on how they will apply what they have learned when reading challenging poems in the future.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003ELearning Outcomes\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EThe sequence of prompts and questions in this activity guide students to develop the following dispositions of proficient readers: \u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E- a capacity for sustained, focused attention\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E- a willingness to suspend closure and entertain multiple interpretations\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E- a tolerance for ambiguity and uncertainty leading to a willingness to reread and reread again\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E- an appreciation for alternative interpretations and visions, and a willingness to change one’s mind\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EMore Lessons Like This One\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003Cbr \u002F\u003EThis is the \u003Cstrong\u003EPDF &amp; Easel for TpT™ version for poetry\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cp\u003EThis resource is also available in three other versions:\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\u003Cul\u003E\u003Cli\u003E\u003Ca
